 aise main ek aisa plateform jahaan khabaron kii duniya se lekar, vyapaar, arth, raajnneeti, or shiksha jaise tamaam peshey se jude log twitor kaa istemaal karte hai
 They may have to be two or four times porn-untested anytime
 ye bahut had tak mumkin he ki kisi kshetra vishesh main porn websites ko bain kiya ja saktaa he
 But Twitter is a social media platform where porn is openly available, but it cannot be banned by declaring it a porn website
 or ise baari taadaad main logon dwaara upyog kiya jaataa he
 It also includes juvenile youth / young women (adults)
 jaraa sochie aise main us daleel kaa kya hoga jo porn websites ko band karte vakt di jaati he
 So the question is whether any government will stop useful platforms like Twitter in any country to keep away from porn
 kyonki twitor kii policy to na jane kab badale yaa shaayad kabhi naa badale

 ye poster is film ke baaki posters kii tarah hi shandaar he

 a senior Doordarshan official has been reported missing from New Delhi area since Friday

 vah baithak main nahin pahunche or unka mobile bhi band he

 unki tasviir sabhi jilon or railway steshnon par bhej die gaye hai

 vah ekaaki or apane kaam main duube rahane vaale the or aisa koi ranjish kaa bhi maamla bhi nahin tha

 pradhanmantri narendra modi ko satta main aae 4 saal or 7 maheene ho chuke hai or is dauraan unhone kai kirtiman bhi banaae hai
 If he visits two countries before the Lok Sabha elections to be held in the next few months, as the Prime Minister, he will become the second Indian Prime Minister to visit the other countries of the world
 indira gandhi ne bataur bhartiya pradhanmantri sabase zyada 113 deshon kii yatraaen kii thi
 As far as Prime Minister Narendra Modi is concerned, he has traveled to a total of 92 countries (including a single visit to the same country) and is behind Manmohan Singh for just one visit
 modi ke purvavarti manmohan singh ne apane pradhanmantritv kaarykaal main 93 deshon (ek hi desh kii dobaaraa yatra bhi shaamil) kii yatraaen kii thi
 However, the major difference between foreign visits between Narendra Modi and Manmohan Singh is that Manmohan Singh traveled to 93 countries during his 2 years of 10 years, whereas Modi has traveled to 92 countries in his four and a half years
 
 jabaki indira gandhi ne apane 15 saal ke kaarykaal ke dauraan 113 deshon kii yatraaen kii thi
 Excess expenditure on chartered flights

 He made his first foreign trip as PM in June 2014
 pradhanmantri modi (5 saal se kam) kii tulana main apane duusare kaarykaal main manmohan singh ke 50 videsh daure ke dauraan 1,350 karod rupee kharch hue the
 This information was given by Minister of State for External Affairs VK Singh in response to a question in Rajya Sabha

 modi ne manmohan singh kii tulana main zyada videsh yatraaen kii or duusare deshon main rahe

 rajyasabha se mantri kii ore se pesh kiye gaye aankadon ke mutabik modi kii videsh yatra par sabase zyada kharch 9 april se 17 april, 2015 tak kii 9 divasiy france, germany or canada kii yatra par aayaa tha

 is hafte film 'bangistan' bhi release hui he, jiske nirdeshak karan anshuman hai
 Ritesh Sidhwani and Farhan Akhtar have produced this film
 mukhya bhoomika main ritesh deshmukh, pulakit samraat, jacleen furnandis, kumud mishra, aryaa babbar, chandan roy sanyaal or tom alter hai
 In this film, there is a fictional country called 'bangistan' where people of two religions want to shake the world by bombing the Sarva Dharma Sammelan happening abroad for their benefit
 ye kaam praveen chaturvedi yani pulkit samraat or hafeez yani ritesh deshmukh ko diya jaataa he or ye pahunch jate hai poland
 For what happens next, you have to buy a movie ticket
 ab baat khoobiyon or khaamiyon kii
 This film is a tinge on the current situation, where many countries are troubled by terrorism and an attempt has been made to make this issue in the film through comedy
 afsos kii ye tanj chehre par muskuraahat nahin laa paata
 You definitely appreciate the idea of writer and director by watching the film, but the film neither laughs nor makes you cry, ie a weak script
 tippaniyan Pulkit has done a lot of loud acting, some scenes of the film are worn out, like Pulkit's Ramlila
 
 
 vahiin kai seens kaa taana buna acha buna gaya he, lekin ye beasar sabit hote hai
 At the same time, the songs of the film are also tight but they do not climb on the tongue
 jacleen kaa film main kuch kaam nahin tha, na hi unka kirdaar asardaar he or na hi unka abhinay
 Now the thing in which the number comes first is the theme of the film, which is amazing
 jis tarah se kahani ko aage badhaayaa gaya he, vah bhi acha he, film kii ek line he - 'jab main tu bana or tu main, tab ham ek duusare ko samaj paae' jo sankshipt main bahut badi baat kah jaati he
 Riteish does justice to his character, the film's screenplay is tight
 film ke bare main yah meraa nazariyaa tha, aapkaa kuch or ho saktaa he, isliye jaaie or film dekhie

 iske saath hi sebi pramukh ajay tyaagi ne kaha he ki companiyon main gadabadi kaa khulaasa karne waalon (wheasal bluers) ke bich bharosa paidaa karne ke liye adhik shaktiyon kii jarurat he
 Sebi needs powers! According to news agency PTI, Sebi chief Ajay Tyagi said that more powers are probably needed to create trust among the whistleblowers (whistle Blowers)
 tyaagi ne iti company infosis ke khilaaf gadabadi ujagar karne vaale ke sebi ke bajaay america niamak esaisi ke paas jane kii prishthbhumi main yah baat kahi

 companiyon ke karj ko lekar paardarshitaavaheen sebi ne listed companiyon ke liye karj nahin chukaa paane kii jaankaree dene sambandhi niyamon ko sakht bana diya he
